**Scene A:**

I predict the red object *will* make contact with the yellow region.

**Scene D:**

It is also less likely to topple than in other cases. I predict the red object will *not* make contact with the yellow region.

Comparing the scenarios, Scene C has the highest probability of success, as the rolling globe makes the stack much more unstable. Scene B is also very likely, as the coffee maker seems prone to toppling. However, given the globe's instability, it is more likely to result in a successful outcome.
